<pics>None</pics><Date>1618068717708</Date><Name>Zach Fry< /Name>< text>
Nice beach with a pier. Lots of room. There are designated surf/swim areas and lifeguards are usually on duty. The surf is dependable here as the sand bottom tends to shift with the moving tide.

Usually, the best time to surf here is in the morning because afternoons can get really windy and make for choppy waves. Works best at mid to high tide.< /text>

< text>
Public beach that‚Äôs usually quiet during the week and busy on weekends. Paved pathway for walking, biking, etc. Lots of surfing, sunbathing and other beach activities. From the beach, I‚Äôve seen passing dolphin pods and the occasional sea lion. Water is usually 60-70 degrees Fahrenheit. Free parking in residential areas bordering beach, but gets busy by late mornings on weekends. See photo of sign for rules and regulations on dogs, no drinking, etc. Overall, a wonderful beach!<//text>

My mother and I love this place! We go here pretty much everytime I can get over to Redondo from San Pedro. From the Ceviche that they set down once you've ordered to fresh grilled fish choices and thru the wonderful sides, we've never been disappointed. And when you think about the price, it's so reasonable compared to an old school fish restaurant. The only problem we have with it is the acoustics. The place is so noisy!! I would look into this as they expand.< /Text>

< text>
Jolene has been our family dentist for over 15 years.
She earned our business then because my son, who was 9 at the time, bit a hard piece of candy that broke his tooth.

She has built an excellent environment and is top notch in my opinion!

I would not consider going to anyone else!!< /text>
